    <h2>Home</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>Home</h3></li>
       <li><a href="/start.html" title="Let’s Get Started">Let’s Get Started</a></li>

    <div id="main"> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <p><img src="/images/main/home/spotlight_02.jpg" alt="" height="230" width="700" /></p> 
      <h3><img src="/images/homepage_begin_ttl.gif" alt="Been tasked with producing a communications project? Not sure where to begin?" width="543" height="47" /></h3> 
      <p class="kicker">Let Creative Designs Services (CDS) be your guide.</p> 
      <p class="kicker">Serving the University Advancement division and institutional executive leadership, our multimedia services team members are skilled at helping colleges and departments produce effective communications projects.</p> 
      <p><a href="mailto:luis.sanz@ucr.edu?subject=Project%20Consultation">Contact Luis Sanz, Creative Director for a free consultation</a>: We look forward to working with you.</p> 
      <p><img src="/images/design6/cold_horiz_rule.gif" alt="" width="700" height="4" /></p> 
      <div class="col3_divided"> 
       <div class="column3"> 
        <h4><img src="/images/tools_you_need_ttl.gif" alt="The tools you need to create a great project" width="220" height="160" /></h4> 
        <p>When representing UC Riverside, it is important that you use the correct university logos and abide by its standards for design. <a class="standout3" href="/standards.html">We can help</a></p> 
        <h4 class="section"><img src="/images/getting_started_ttl.gif" alt="Getting Started" width="220" height="119" /></h4> 
        <p>Starting a communications project with Creative Design Services? <a class="standout3" href="/start.html">Here are the steps to follow</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="column23R"> 
        <h4><img src="/images/services_offered_ttl.gif" alt="The Services We Offer. CDS is a full-service design studio, offering:" width="307" height="42" /></h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Complete project coordination—from concept development to final print. </li> 
         <li>Design and coordination of the print production of 
          <ul class="col"> 
           <li>Magazines </li> 
           <li>Brochures </li> 
           <li>Posters </li> 
           <li>Newsletters </li> 
           <li>Invitations </li> 
           <li>Banners </li> 
           <li>Flyers </li> 
          </ul> <br class="endcol" /></li> 
         <li>Original illustrations and drawings for publications. </li> 
         <li>Technical illustrations for graphs, charts, diagrams and maps. </li> 
        </ul> 
        <p><img src="/images/design6/col23_horiz_rule.gif" alt=" " width="460" height="4" /></p> 
        <div id="box">
         <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/bkgrnd_top.png" alt="" width="440" height="83" /> 
         <h3 class="accessibility">An integrated Approach Office of Strategic Communications</h3> 
         <ul id="ul_puzzle"> 
          <li><a id="a_intro" title="Introduction" href="#div_intro"></a></li> 
          <!--li><a id="a_cds" title="Creative Design Services" href="#div_cds"></a></li--> 
          <li><a id="a_marketing" title="Marketing" href="#div_marketing"></a></li> 
          <li><a id="a_media" title="Media Relations" href="#div_media"></a></li> 
          <li><a id="a_video" title="Video Production" href="#div_video"></a></li> 
          <li><a id="a_web" title="Web Development" href="#div_web"></a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <div id="div_intro"> 
          <p><strong>The departments within</strong> the Office of Strategic Communications work together to promote you and your university.</p> 
         </div> 
         <!--div id="div_cds"--> 
         <!-- xcom.omniupdate.div label="cds" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
         <!--p><strong>From conception to delivery</strong>, UCR’s award-winning in-house design team help colleges and departments produce communication projects that tell your story to the world.</p>
<p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_orange.png" alt="" width="80" height="72" /><a class="standout3" href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/">Visit the Creative Design Services site</a></p--> 
         <!--/div--> 
         <div id="div_marketing"> 
          <p><strong>From advertising to publications</strong>, creative development to market research, the Marketing team is responsible for developing and implementing integrated marketing strategies that enhance the university’s image and reputation.</p> 
          <p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_red.png" alt="" width="80" height="72" /><a class="standout3" href="http://marketing.ucr.edu/">Visit the Marketing site</a></p> 
         </div> 
         <div id="div_media"> 
          <p><strong>The Media Relations team</strong> communicates with media around the world to spread the news about what is happening at UC Riverside. They are also responsible for several publications, including <cite>UCR Magazine</cite> and <cite>Inside UCR</cite>.</p> 
          <p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_purple.png" alt="" width="88" height="73" /><a class="standout3" href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/">Visit the Media Relations site</a></p> 
         </div> 
         <div id="div_video"> 
          <p><strong>UCR’s primary source</strong> for original video and television programming. It’s facilities have full post-production capabilities and are a vast resource of the campus and the Inland Southern California community.</p> 
          <p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_yellow.png" alt="" width="80" height="72" /><a class="standout3" href="http://videoproduction.ucr.edu/">Visit the Video Production site</a></p> 
         </div> 
         <div id="div_web"> 
          <p><strong>The Web Development</strong> team is responsible for the design and upkeep of the award-winning UCR “Umbrella” website as well as oversight of the university’s overall online presence.</p> 
          <p><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/puzzle_blue.png" alt="" width="80" height="72" /><a class="standout3" href="http://webdevelopment.ucr.edu/">Visit the Web Development site</a></p> 
         </div> 
         <img class="border_image_bottom" src="/images/box/bkgrnd_bottom.png" alt="" width="440" height="9" /> 
         <div class="clear"></div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

             <div class="body-wrap">
              <h3 class="fw-b fz-s lh-115"><a class="" href="http://news.yahoo.com/anti-fracking-activist-barred-40-percent-pennsylvania-county-213256111--finance.html" data-ylk="sec:strm;cat:default;bpos:1;cpos:2;pkgt:4;slk:title;ct:1;rspns:nav;">Anti-fracking activist barred from visiting friends, grocery store</a></h3>
              <p class="summary mt-xxs">By David DeKok HARRISBURG, Pennsylvania (Reuters) - A court injunction obtained by Texas-based Cabot Oil &amp; Gas is preventing Pennsylvania resident Vera Scroggins from going to her local grocery store, her friends' homes, schools, or even the hospital. That's because those properties sit atop the more than 200,000 acres in Susquehanna County that the energy producer owns and leases for gas extraction - land on which Scroggins, a determined anti-fracking activist, is not allowed to tread. A judge in October granted Cabot's request to bar Scroggins from the land - more than 40 percent of Susquehanna County, where she lives - after her repeated trespassing, court documents show. Her offending actions included giving a tour last year to anti-drilling celebrities Susan Sarandon, Yoko Ono, and Sean Lennon, the documents said.</p>

              <p class="summary mt-xxs">A public row erupted Tuesday between the CIA and the US lawmakers who oversee its intelligence work, with the agency's director angrily denying claims it spied on Senate staff. Senate Intelligence Committee chair Dianne Feinstein launched an attack on the Central Intelligence Agency, accusing it of searching computers used by staffers investigating CIA interrogation methods. &quot;I have grave concerns that the CIA's search may well have violated the separation of powers principles embodied in the United States Constitution,&quot; Feinstein declared on the Senate floor. She alleged that the CIA may have violated federal law as well as an executive order that bars it from domestic spying, but the agency's director John Brennan quickly denied the allegations.</p>

Survivors bowed deeply and joined hands at remembrance ceremonies in towns and cities around the disaster zone and in Tokyo, where Emperor Akihito and Empress Michiko led tributes to those who died in Japan's worst peace-time disaster. Giant waves also crashed into the Fukushima nuclear plant, sparking reactor meltdowns and explosions, and setting off the worst atomic crisis in a generation. As night fell, an event in a Fukushima park saw about 2,000 lit candles arranged to read &quot;Fukushima 3/11&quot;.</p>

      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

                    $(this).attr({
                    "src" : url + "&wmode=transparent",
                    "wmode" : "Opaque"});
                }

  <script type="text/javascript">
            // Takes the full URL and reduces to only path, and file name sans extension.
            function cleanHREF(href, extension){
              // Found RE on StackOverflow:
              // http://stackoverflow.com/questions/27745/getting-parts-of-a-url-regex)
              var uri_regex = /^((http[s]?|ftp):\/)?\/?([^:\/\s]+)(:([^\/]*))?((\/\w+)*\/)([\w\-\.]+[^#?\s]+)(\?([^#]*))?(#(.*))?$/;
              var clean_href = href.toString();
              //Regex returns array with indexes as follows:
              var SCHEMA = 2, DOMAIN = 3, PORT = 5, PATH = 6,
              FILE = 8, QUERYSTRING = 9, HASH = 12;
              var match_container = clean_href.match(uri_regex)
            
              return match_container[PATH] + match_container[FILE].replace(extension, '');
            }
            
            function stripHTTP(href){
                return href.replace('https?://','');
            }
    
        	
            $(document).ready(function() {
                $('[href$=".xls"],[href$=".pdf"],[href$=".doc"],[href$=".ppt"],[href$=".mp4"],[href$=".flv"],[href$=".png"],[href$=".swf"],.googleDocLink,.GoogleAnalytics_Trackable').click(function(){
                    _gat._getTracker('UA-27780401-1')._trackPageview(escape(stripHTTP($(this).attr('href'))));
                });
            });	
        </script>

         <h2> UC DELIVERS </h2> 
         <div class="spotlightstory"> 
          <div class="spottext">
            How do we help young people understand and effectively participate in the political and social processes and institutions that shape our society? How do we prepare and encourage youth to become engaged, competent civic leaders? In response to the events of September 11, 2001, there is increased national attention to these questions. Researchers, educators and others need to identify effective strategies for engaging diverse youth in their communities and preparing them for active citizenship. 
           <p><a href="?impact=110&amp;a=52104">Read about: 4-H Youth Development: Fostering Civic Engagement</a> | <a href="http://ucanr.edu/delivers">View Other Stories</a></p> 
          </div> 
          <div class="clearspot"></div> 
         </div> 
         <h2>ESPA&Ntilde;OL</h2>

    <h1><a href="/">UC RIVERSIDE PRESENTS</a></h1> 
    <h2>VOICES OF CHANGE: A free series dedicated to the lively exploration of art, artist, and self, one event at a time.</h2>

    <div class="text"> 
     <h3>Josh Kornbluth, comic monologuist and filmmaker - April 21</h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p><strong><img src="http://media.tumblr.com/tumblr_mbmxoeNfqJ1rxdq17.jpg" /></strong></p> 
      <p><strong><a href="http://www.joshkornbluth.com/" title="Josh Kornbluth">JOSH KORNBLUTH</a>: THE MATHEMATICS OF CHANGE</strong></p> 
      <p>A comic monologue that recounts the uproarious experiences of a Princeton University would-be math whiz who discovers his limits in freshman calculus.&nbsp;</p> 
      <p>April 21, 2013, 4pm<br /><span><a href="http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu" title="Culver Center of the Arts">Culver Center of the Arts</a>&nbsp;- 3834 Main Street, Riverside <br /></span><span>Free <span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;</span></span></p> 
      <p><a href="http://maps.google.com/maps?hl=en&amp;gl=us&amp;daddr=3834+Main+Street,+Riverside,+CA+92501&amp;panel=1&amp;f=d&amp;fb=1&amp;dirflg=d&amp;geocode=0,33.981264,-117.374450&amp;cid=0,0,875492350631520353&amp;hq=culver+center+of+the+arts&amp;hnear=0x80dca6df7ff47dbb:0xf7a1d705135e0ae8,Riverside,+CA&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=6FB0UPr_NsjRiAL_xoCICA&amp;ved=0CHUQngIwAA%20" title="map view">map</a></p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function(){
        var analytics_frame = document.getElementById('ga_target');
        var analytics_iframe_loaded;
        var user_logged_in;
        var blog_is_nsfw = 'No';

        var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? "addEventListener" : "attachEvent";
        var eventer = window[eventMethod];
        var messageEvent = eventMethod == "attachEvent" ? "onmessage" : "message";
        eventer(messageEvent,function(e) {
            var message = (e.data && e.data.split) ? e.data.split(';') : '';
            switch (message[0]) {
                case 'analytics_iframe_loaded':
                    analytics_iframe_loaded = true;
                    postCSMessage();
                    postGAMessage();
                    break;
                case 'user_logged_in':
                    user_logged_in = message[1];
                    postGAMessage();
                    break;
            }
        }, false);

        analytics_frame.src = "http://assets.tumblr.com/analytics.html?dc636e9b34dfd27b194aed14513506cb#http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com"
        function postGAMessage() {
            if (analytics_iframe_loaded && user_logged_in) {
                var is_ajax = false;
                analytics_frame.contentWindow.postMessage(['tick_google_analytics', is_ajax, user_logged_in, blog_is_nsfw, '/post/33237316323/josh-kornbluth-comic-monologuist-and-filmmaker-april?route=%2Fpost%2F%3Aid%2F%3Asummary'].join(';'), analytics_frame.src.split('/analytics.html')[0]);
            }
        }
        function postCSMessage() {
            COMSCORE = true;
            analytics_frame.contentWindow.postMessage('enable_comscore;' + window.location, analytics_frame.src.split('/analytics.html')[0]);
        }
    })();
</script>

        if (Tumblr.FollowTeaser && Tumblr.PostMessageListener) {
            // Don't do anything until the first initialize event
            Tumblr.PostMessageListener.initialize(function(message, origin) {
